#
#	Unity Polygon Packing is very space efficient
#	It also trims transparent borders pixels 
#	This information is ditched and not imported in Unity
#	Illarions item table has offsets relying on the exact size of the image
#	Due to the trimming the offset is wrong
#	This file contains the trimmed pixels to each borders
#	So the offset table data can be updated
#
#	name, is trimmed?, trimmed left, trimmed top, trimmed right, trimmed bottom
#
